Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 2-rules system (2 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TRFC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 12-rules system (12 strict rules).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 11-rules system (11 strict rules).
Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
Remains to prove termination of a 34-rules system (23 strict rules).
Removing 5 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 29-rules system (18 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 183-rules system (54 strict rules).
Removing 52 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 131-rules system (36 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 1077-rules system (130 strict rules).
Removing 394 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 683-rules system (72 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 6109-rules system (282 strict rules).
Removing 2370 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 3739-rules system (144 strict rules).
Removing 3040 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 699-rules system (0 strict rules).
QED
